\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Please state the following reasonings for building the model:}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    1) your choice of non\PYZhy{}linear activation function (choice from ‘sigmoid’, ‘tanh’, ‘relu’ and etc).}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Because sigmoid and tanh are almost flat away from the center, }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}they would need a high learning rate for deeper layers. Since I don\PYZsq{}t know or set the learning rate here, }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}I used RELU.}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    2) your choice of the loss function for back\PYZhy{}propagation}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}The labels are 10 catagories, not encoded in one\PYZhy{}hot I used multi\PYZhy{}class catagorical cross entropy}
         
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    3) your choice of the optimizer (‘sgd’, ‘adagra’, ‘adam’ and etc.). You can start with the default learning}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}rate with the optimizer of your choice.  }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}This part can be completed by using the mathematical reasonings or }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}the experiments results between different choices of the model structure. }
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}adagrad is for spase data, where some labels  are much rarer than others. }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}That is not the case with fashion MNST. Also learning rate can get too small, }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}but my NN are probably to shallow for this to matter}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}RMSprop is for recurant NN, which this is not.}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}sgd helps to avoid local minimum.}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}adam is simillar, but \PYZsq{}slows\PYZsq{} the occilation of SGD by useing mean and variance.}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}It \PYZdq{} is straightforward to implement, is computationally efficient, }
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}has little memory requirements, is invariant to diagonal rescaling of the gradients,  is straightforward to implement, is computationally efficient, has little memory requirements, is invariant to diagonal rescaling of the gradients, and is well suited for problems that are large in terms of data and/or parameters.}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}and is well suited for problems that are large in terms of data and/or parameters.\PYZdq{}}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}so I used ADAM}
\end{Verbatim}

None
model 1,2 hidden layers of 64 relu, has 55,050. The first layer just takes the input and makes it a 1D array.
the first hidden layer has a parameter for all of these 784 input for each of the 64 nodes.
the second hidden layer learns a weight for each of the 64 in the prior node for each of the 64 in this layer
the final soft max layer has 10 nodes to give a probability for each catagory. These each have a parameter to each of the prior nodes

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
model1 has a test accuracy of  0.8654 \%
model2 has a test accuracy of  0.8609 \%
the validiation accuracy was \textasciitilde{}87.4\%, so this is still a bit overfit. In theory it should be less overfit.
As for the prior case, the large network did better and here it is not much worse, I wonder if I have too few nodes to begin with. That would already avoid overfitting, and then droping more would just make things worse?

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}166}]:} \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{QUESTION 3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    3. Convolutional neural network (CNN) (7 pts)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}In this section, you will build a convolutional neural network with the architecture of your choice.}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}The focus will not be put on hyper\PYZhy{}parameter tuning since the computation burden is high for a personal computer. }
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}You will use the same set of validation data as in part 2 to monitor your training process.}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}A sample architecture of a convolutional neural network:}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Conv2D \PYZhy{} MaxPooling2D \PYZhy{} Conv2D \PYZhy{} MaxPooling2D – Flatten – Dense – Dense(output layer)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Note:}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}You can simplify this architecture if you feel the computation is too slow in your computer.}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}You can also add more fancy architecture to achieve a better performance if you have good computation resources.}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}The reported performance of the training will not be used as the grading criteria.}
          
          
          \PY{n}{modelc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{keras}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
              \PY{n}{keras}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Conv2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{32}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strides}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}

          	\PY{n+nd}{@staticmethod}
          	\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{build}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{width}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{height}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{depth}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{classes}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
          		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} initialize the model along with the input shape to be}
          		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}channels last\PYZdq{} and the channels dimension itself}
          		\PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
          		\PY{n}{inputShape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{height}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{width}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{depth}\PY{p}{)}
          		\PY{n}{chanDim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
           
          		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} if we are using \PYZdq{}channels first\PYZdq{}, update the input shape}

          		\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{K}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{image\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{channels\PYZus{}first}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}

          		\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Conv2D}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{32}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{padding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{same}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}

          		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} first (and only) set of FC =\PYZgt{} RELU layers}
          		\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          		\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{512}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

          		\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{BatchNormalization}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

          		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} softmax classifier}
          		\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{classes}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

          		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} return the constructed network architecture}
          		\PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{model}

          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} import the necessary packages}

          \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{datasets} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{fashion\PYZus{}mnist}
          \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{utils} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{np\PYZus{}utils}
          \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{keras} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{backend} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{K}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}from imutils import build\PYZus{}montages}
          \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{matplotlib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{pyplot} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{plt}
          \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{numpy} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{np}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}import cv2}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} initialize the number of epochs to train for, base learning rate,}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} and batch size}
          \PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}EPOCHS} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{25}
          \PY{n}{INIT\PYZus{}LR} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}2}
          \PY{n}{BS} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{32}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} grab the Fashion MNIST dataset (if this is your first time running}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this the dataset will be automatically downloaded)}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{[INFO] loading Fashion MNIST...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{trainX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{trainY}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{testY}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{fashion\PYZus{}mnist}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} if we are using \PYZdq{}channels first\PYZdq{} ordering, then reshape the design}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} matrix such that the matrix is:}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 	num\PYZus{}samples x depth x rows x columns}
          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{K}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{image\PYZus{}data\PYZus{}format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{channels\PYZus{}first}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}
          	\PY{n}{trainX} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{trainX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{trainX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          	\PY{n}{testX} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{testX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} otherwise, we are using \PYZdq{}channels last\PYZdq{} ordering, so the design}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} matrix shape should be: num\PYZus{}samples x rows x columns x depth}
          \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
          	\PY{n}{trainX} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{trainX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{trainX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          	\PY{n}{testX} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{testX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} scale data to the range of [0, 1]}
          \PY{n}{trainX} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{trainX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{float32}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mf}{255.0}
          \PY{n}{testX} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{testX}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{float32}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mf}{255.0}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} one\PYZhy{}hot encode the training and testing labels}
          \PY{n}{trainY} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np\PYZus{}utils}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}categorical}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{trainY}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{testY} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np\PYZus{}utils}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}categorical}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testY}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} initialize the label names}
          \PY{n}{labelNames} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{top}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{trouser}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{pullover}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{dress}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{coat}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
          	\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{sandal}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{shirt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{sneaker}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{bag}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ankle boot}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} initialize the optimizer and model}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{[INFO] compiling model...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{opt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{SGD}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lr}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{INIT\PYZus{}LR}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{momentum}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.9}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decay}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{INIT\PYZus{}LR} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}EPOCHS}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{MiniVGGNet}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{build}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{width}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{height}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{depth}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{classes}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{categorical\PYZus{}crossentropy}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{opt}\PY{p}{,}
          	\PY{n}{metrics}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{accuracy}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} train the network}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{[INFO] training model...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{H} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{trainX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{trainY}\PY{p}{,}
          	\PY{n}{validation\PYZus{}data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{testY}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
          	\PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{BS}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}EPOCHS}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} make predictions on the test set}
          \PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testX}\PY{p}{)}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} show a nicely formatted classification report}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{[INFO] evaluating network...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{classification\PYZus{}report}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testY}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argmax}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{preds}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argmax}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
          	\PY{n}{target\PYZus{}names}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{labelNames}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
           
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} plot the training loss and accuracy}
          \PY{n}{N} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{NUM\PYZus{}EPOCHS}
          \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{style}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{use}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ggplot}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{figure}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}201}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Answer the following questions regarding your model training:}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    1) The number parameters of each layer (use model.summary()). }
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Compare the result with the fully connected neural network. State the advantage of the CNN.}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{the CNN}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{summary}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{the smallest/best test accuracy model:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model1}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{summary}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{as the CNN does not have the layers take all values as input, but only a small neighborhood, it will have to learn fewer paramters per layer. However, here it has many more layers}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    2) Plot the learning curve (training  and validation loss versus the epoch; training  and validation accuracy versus the epoch). State whether you have observed overfitting. Report the test accuracy.}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{from the curves seen above, it does not appear overfit noticiably. The loss for validation becomes worse than training after epoch 15. But this is barely noticable.}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    3) (optional +3 points) State whether you faced the overfitting problem and propose the possible workaround. Experiment with your proposed method and add the learning curve to the plot of 2). Report the test accuracy.}
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{I trained for relativly few epochs, so this probably helped me avoid overfitting. Other ways to avoid overfitting are by having a small network, regulrization penelties on the parameters, and drop out so only random subsets of nodes are trained each epoch.}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}    
          \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{the test accuracy above is in the table/matrix above. For some catagories it is better, but averages to 93}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Save your choice of the trained model into a HDF5 file and submit it with your report. }
          \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{save}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{my\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}CNN.h5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_
None
as the CNN does not have the layers take all values as input, but only a small neighborhood, it will have to learn fewer paramters per layer. However, here it has many more layers
from the curves seen above, it does not appear overfit noticiably. The loss for validation becomes worse than training after epoch 15. But this is barely noticable.
I trained for relativly few epochs, so this probably helped me avoid overfitting. Other ways to avoid overfitting are by having a small network, regulrization penelties on the parameters, and drop out so only random subsets of nodes are trained each epoch.
the test accuracy above is in the table/matrix above. For some catagories it is better, but averages to 93\%
